name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted July 23, 2023
msg:Feature 1 Comes with 9 private islands and future water world
The hotel has its own island and water world domineeringly, so that guests can have a good time without leaving the hotel.
There are two lighthouses in Qiandao Lake, one is in the Intercontinental Hotel on the Xianshan Peninsula, and the other is in the beer town. There is a chain bridge built on the southeast side of the main island of Keren Hotel. Guests walking on the bridge can look at the internet celebrity lighthouse in Beer Town from afar.
After crossing the bridge, you can come to the natural island to explore. The passages between the islands are paved with red stones. The island originally had a vegetable garden, an orchard and a mini zoo. It is a pity that because the water level of Qiandao Lake is high now, the passage is submerged by the lake, and it is impossible to walk there. It is a pity that we can only look at the ponies on the island in the distance.
Fortunately, the vegetation on the island is lush, and you won't feel bored while walking. The hotel has set up a wooden maze for children, a "wooden structure expansion area" and a "plum blossom pile", which children can explore. Telescopes are set up on the island, and tourists can look at the hot air balloons, paragliders and occasional flying birds in the sky.
If you like water sports, you can go to the hotel's own water world to play and kayak at your own expense. Because the weather is really hot, we didn't experience it.
the
Feature 2 Infinity Pool
In the hot summer, enjoying the beautiful scenery of Qiandao Lake by the pool is the most pleasant. The scenery is invincible, as if you are swimming between heaven and earth, and you feel comfortable. Sometimes swimming is more about the environment and more about the state of mind.
the
Feature 3 Unique design with humanistic feelings
The hotel is not grand and bright in the traditional sense, but secretive and low-key. It is said to be designed by Singaporean and Japanese designers. The overall color is the dark red of the Qiandao Lake soil. The shore is built with brick-red stones of the same color. The arc-shaped building surfaces make each room directly face the Qiandao Lake. The atrium of the hotel is particularly delicate at night. The scattered lamp beads are reflected on the transparent floor-to-ceiling windows, scattered as "fireflies", and the low-key dim yellow makes the night more peaceful. Ingenuity is seen in the details, and even the signs spell out a pleasant word "ke".
At the same time, the hotel is willing to use the public space as a book bar, a wine house, a collection room, and a children's activity room. The a**osphere is warm and comfortable, full of sincerity. The hotel also has a self-service laundry room. You can wash and dry after swimming. The dryer is really useful.
the
Feature 4 Daily little surprises
Small surprises are prepared for the guests every day during the stay: when you check in, you will get a Parma water toiletry set and electric toothbrush, and in the evening, you will get fruit snacks and sachets. Even a small mirror in the room is Chanel. At breakfast the next day, there will be photographers waiting to take family photos for the guests, and a box of fresh seasonal vegetables grown by themselves will be given as a gift when leaving the store. In short, every day let the guests feel the care of the hotel.
the
Feature 5: Semi-buffet breakfast
Breakfast is not a traditional full buffet, but a staple food set plus drinks, snacks and fruit buffet. You can choose one of four main dishes for the set meal, including flounder, fried noodles, wontons and rice balls. There is also a set meal, including hard-boiled eggs, porridge, side dishes, fried dumplings and pastries. It is healthy and clean, and can be full. However, there is no picture of the menu for reference when the guest chooses the staple food, so they can only choose blindly. Therefore, it is suggested that the hotel design a graphic menu, which is more intuitive. Children's meals are relatively simple, consisting of thin chocolate toast, cheese sticks and hard-boiled eggs. Children are usually not full, so they need to go to the self-service area to get some small bread and fruit. Children like dried fruit very much. I like longan and red date tea the most. There is a 50¬∞ warm coaster to keep it warm. Drink it to warm your stomach.
the
Naturally, the hotel also has its shortcomings:
Disadvantage 1: The contradiction between design and practicality
Beautiful design sometimes comes at the expense of practicality. For example, although the appearance of the hotel is chic, the space structure is not closed, and the corridors are all open-air. Walking outside in summer will feel extremely stuffy.
the
Disadvantage 2: There are no restaurants around
The price of meals in the hotel is expensive, and there are only farmhouses around. The funny thing is, the residents of our same restaurant met at a nearby fish restaurant by appoin**ent, and they ate ordinary farm food, and the price was not cheap. The nearby Yintai City Ferris Wheel has been erected, but it has not yet opened.
